1a1(rgyud): rabs rdo rje sems pa'i rlung ba zhums s+ho//
2a1(rgyud): shrI gu h+ya sa dza tan+t+ra ra dza/ bod skad
2a2(rgyud): du/ rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal gsang ba 'dus
2b1(rgyud): pa/ dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gi thos
2b2(rgyud): 'dus pacagadam da pa na gagags pa rnams kyi lhu
2b3(rgyud): dang thugs kyi snying po rdo rje btsun mo'i b+ha ga la/ brjod kyis mi lang ba'i yang brjod
3a1(rgyud): kyis mi yang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul phra rab snyed kyi/ byang chub
3a2(rgyud): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po la 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
3a3(rgyud): dam tshig rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen sku rdo rje dang / byang chub sems
3a4(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' chen po gsung rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' chen po thugs rdo rje dang /
3b1(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ting nge 'dzin rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dang
3b2(rgyud): chen po rgyal ba rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos rdo rje dang / byang chub sems
3b3(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' chen po chu rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mo rdo rje dang / byung
3b4(rgyud): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rlung rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam
3b5(rgyud): mkha' rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gzugs rdo rje dang / byang chub sem
4a1(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' chen po smra rdo rdo dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po da
4a2(rgyud): dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ro rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po reg bya rdo rje
4a3(rgyud): dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos dbyings ngo bo nyid dang / de dag la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa'
4a4(rgyud): sems dpa' chen po brjod kyis mi lang ba'i yang dag brjod kyi mi lang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing na rdul phra rab snyed rnams dang / de
4a5(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa na mkha'i dbyings dang mnyam pa la/ 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa mi bskyod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs
4a6(rgyud): pa rdo rje rnam par snang mdzad dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen dpal dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje 'od dpag tu med pa
4b1(rgyud): dang / de bzhin gshegs rdo rje gdon mi za ba dang / de dag la sogs pa na mkha'i dbyings thams cad dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams dang
4b2(rgyud): thabs gcig tu bzhugs pa ni 'di lta ste/ dper na til gyi gang bu bzhin du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis na mkha'i dbyings thams cad rab
4b3(rgyud): tu gang bar snang bar gyur to// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje rnam par snang mdzad chen po/ de bzhin gshegs pa
4b4(rgyud): thams cad kyi 'dod chags chen po'i tshul zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bkod pa de dag thams cad nyid
4b5(rgyud): kyi sku la zhugs par mdzad do/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad kyis/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang /
4b6(rgyud): gsung dang / thugs kyi bdag po yongasu mnyes par bya ba'i phyir nyid kyi sku bud med kyi gzugasu mngon par sprul nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang
4b7(rgyud): mdzad chen pos sku las mngon par byung bar gyur to// de la la la ni sangs rgyas spyan la bu/ la la ma mA ki si bu/ la la gos dkar mo lta bu/ la ya das
5a1(rgyud): @#tshig sgrol ma lta bu/ la la ni gzugs kyi ngo bo lta bu/ la la sgra'i ngo bo lta bu/ la la dri'i ngo bo lta bu/ la la ro'i ngo bo lta bu/ la la reg gi ngo bo lta bu/
5a2(rgyud): der yang dag par gnas par gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mi bskyod pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi snying po rdo rje btsun
5a3(rgyud): mo'i b+ha ga la/ dam tshig chen po'i dkyil 'khor rdal med pa gru bzhir byin gyis brlabs pa ni/ gsal ba de'i ngo bo nyid/ sna tshogs gzugs kyi kun tu rgyas// sad+yas sprin gyi/
5a4(rgyud): kun tu khyab/ 'od zer 'phro ba mang po 'khrug/ gsol ba la sogs dkyil 'khor ldan/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i kun gyi gnas// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
5a5(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i bdag po// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor chen po'i dbusu bzhig par gyur to// de nas de bzhin
5a6(rgyud): gshegs pa mi bskyed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen dpal dang / de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag tu med pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gdon mi za bar grub pa dang
5a7(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad rnams/ de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi sems rdo rje'i thugs la bzhug so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
5a8(rgyud): byang chub kyi sems rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugaso// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa/
5b1(rgyud): thams cad kyi bdag po snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu/ de nas na mkha'i dbyings 'di thams cad/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i ngo bor gnas par gyur to// de nas
5b2(rgyud): na mkha'i dbyings thams cad na gnas pa'i sems can ji snyed pa de dag thams cad rdo rje sems dpa'i byin gyis brlabs kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bde ba dang /
5b3(rgyud): yid bde ba thob par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi sems rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i
5b4(rgyud): dam tshig 'byung ba'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhags nas/ rig pa chen po skyes bu'i gzugs 'di de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngags kyi byin gyis brlang
5b5(rgyud): kyis/ byin gyis brlab so// byin gyis brlabs ma thag tu bcom ldan 'das byang chub kyi sems rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa de nyid/ zhal gsum pa lta bur de bzhin gshegs pa tham
5b6(rgyud): cad kyis gzigs par gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mi bskyod pa la sogs pa bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyis thugs kha nas byung ste/ ched du brjod pa 'di ched du
5b7(rgyud): brjod do// me ma ho sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ byang chub sems las rab byung ba// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gsang / rab tu mi rtog gnas med pa'o// de nas bcom ldan
5b8(rgyud): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang gcig tu 'dus nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi sems rdo rje la/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
6a1(rgyud): mcho ga spros pa'i khon nyid kyi dam tshigadan po che'i smin gyis yang dgage pa mchod de/ phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces gsol to// 'dus pa gas
6a2(rgyud): ba las byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gsang / rdo rje snying po 'dus pa yi// de nyid bcom ldan bshad du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gtso
6a3(rgyud): ba byang chub kyi sems rdo rjes/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad leg so// leg so// 'on
6a4(rgyud): kyang 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyang the tshom skye bar byed pa yin na/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams lta ci smos/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tham
6a5(rgyud): cad kyi ngo mtsher du gyur rmad du gyur te/ the tshom thams cad gcod par mdzad pa/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po la 'di skad ces gsol to// gang
6a6(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das 'di lta bu'i yon tan khyad par can du gyur pa yang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang /
6a7(rgyud): thugs kyi gsang ba ston par mi spro ba de/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la byin gyis brlabs par mdzad de/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i de
6a8(rgyud): tshigs 'byung ba'i tshig gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bde ba dang / yid bde ba myong bar bgyi ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes dang / mngon pa
6b1(rgyud): shes pa'i 'bras bu thob par bgyi ba'i bar gyi phyir yang dag par bstan du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thug
6b2(rgyud): rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsol ba btab pa de mkhyen nas/ ye shes kyi sgron ma rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhug/
6b3(rgyud): te zhe sdang gi rigs kyi mchog snying po'i snying po 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // badz+ra d+hi ka/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ de bcom ldan 'das de
6b4(rgyud): bzhin gshegs ba thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi reg pa skyes bu de nyid// mi bskyod pa'i phyag rgya chen por sbyor ba'i thabs kyis/ nag po dkar po dmar po'i
6b5(rgyud): tshul du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje la bzhug so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gsheg
6b6(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi dam tshig 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ gti mug gi rigs mchog gi snying po 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo/
6b7(rgyud): rje las byung ngo // dzi na dzi ka/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu/ rna
6b8(rgyud): bar rtswa'i mad byag rgya chen par myur ba'i babs kyis// dkar brdeg pa ngas ba'i tshul du/ de bzhin gzhags pa khas pa cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / zug pa/
7a1(rgyud): ya #las spyan sngar bzhag so// de nas bcom ldan 'das des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rin po che 'byung ba'i rdo rje dpal zhes bya ba'i ting
7a2(rgyud): 'dzin la snyoms par zhags te/ yid bzhin nor bu'i rigs mchog kyi snying po 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // rad na d+hi ka/ de nas 'di phyung ma
7a3(rgyud): zag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi reg pa'i skyes bu/ rin chen dpal gyi rgya chen por sbyor bas/ na mkha'i gnas kyis/
7a4(rgyud): ser po nag po dkar po'i tshul du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i lho phyogasu bzhug so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
7a5(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi 'dod chags chen po 'byung ba'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ rdo rje 'dod chags kyi rigs mchog gi snying po'i snying po 'di nyid
7a6(rgyud): kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // a ro li ka/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang /
7a7(rgyud): thugs rig pa'i skyes bu/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi rig pa'i dag po phyag rgya chen por sbyor ba'i thabs kyis/ dmar po nag po dkar po'i tshul du/ de bzhin gshegs pa tham
7a8(rgyud): cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i rgyab tu bzhug so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gdon mi za pa'i mchog dam tshig 'byung
7b1(rgyud): rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ dam tshig 'gug pa'i rigs mchog gi snying po 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byung ngo / prad dzA d+hAka
7b2(rgyud): de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rigs pa'i skyes bu/ grub pa gdon mi za ba'i phyag chen
7b3(rgyud): bor sbyor ba'i thabs kyis/ ljang khu nag po dkar po'i tshul du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje yi byang phyogasu bzhag so// // zhe
7b4(rgyud): sdang gti mug 'dod chags dang // yid bzhin nor bu'i dam tshig ste// rigs lngar gtogs pa 'di rnams kyis// 'dod dang thar pa rab bsgrub pa'o// / de nas yang
7b5(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje 'dzin rje su mnyes par byed pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ rdo rje 'dzin thams cad
7b6(rgyud): kyi btsun mo'i mchog 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las byung ngo // de shar ti/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tham
7b7(rgyud): cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu/ de nyid bud med kyi gzugs 'dzin par 'gyur te/ bden bral gyi grwar bzhug so// // de nas bcom ldan 'ad
7b8(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rjesu mnyes par byed pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi btsun mo'i mcho//
8a1(rgyud): 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // mo ha ra ti/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi/
8a2(rgyud): sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu de nyid/ bud med kyi gzugs 'dzin par 'gyur te/ me'i 'tsham su bzhugaso// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gsheg
8a3(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi 'dod chags 'dzin pa/ rjesu chags par byed pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'dod chags
8a4(rgyud): 'dzin pa btsun ma'i mchog 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung // rA ga ra ti/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams
8a5(rgyud): kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu de nyid/ bud med kyi gzugs 'dzin par 'gyur te/ nub phyogs kyi grwar bzhugaso// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de
8a6(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs slu ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi shes
8a7(rgyud): rab 'chang ba'i mchog btsun mo 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // badz+ra ra ti/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
8a8(rgyud): cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu de nyid bud med kyi gzugs 'dzin par gyur te/ byang phyogs kyi grwar bzhug so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi/
8b1(rgyud): btsun mo'i mchog phun sum tshogs pa'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad rdo rje 'khor lo zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshes
8b2(rgyud): thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i khro bo chen po 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // ya man ta krid/ de nas de phyung ma thag
8b3(rgyud): tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rig pa'i skyes bu de nyid/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snyengs par byed
8b4(rgyud): pa'i tshul du/ shar phyogs kyi sgor bzhug so// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mngon par byang chub pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la
8b5(rgyud): snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor byin gyis brlob pa zhes bya ba'i khro bo chen po 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las
8b6(rgyud): phyung ngo // pradz+nyA ta krid/ de nas de phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi rigs pa'i skyes bu de nyid/ rdo rje dam
8b7(rgyud): tshig bsgrengs par byed pa'i tshul du/ lho phyogs kyi sgor bzhug so// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos rin po che 'byung gnas rdo rje na
8b8(rgyud): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'dod chags 'chang ba'i dkyil 'khor byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba khro bo chen po 'di nyid kyisgra
9a1(rgyud): dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las byung ngo // pad+ma ta krid/ de nas de phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung
9a2(rgyud): dang / thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu de nyid/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi tshul du/ nub phyogs kyi sgor bzhug so// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
9a3(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ti nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang /
9a4(rgyud): thugs kyi dkyil 'khor byin gyis brlob pa khro bo chen po 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // bag+hin ta krid/ de nas de phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'ang
9a5(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi reg pa'i skyes bu de nyid/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi tshul du/
9a6(rgyud): byang phyogs kyi sgor bzhug so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs mnyes par byed pa dang / dkyil 'khor gyi dam tshig sems dpa' rnams
9a7(rgyud): so// // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ge gsang ba 'dus pa las/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor byin
9a8(rgyud): gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i le'u ste// dang po'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi bdag
9b1(rgyud): po la/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis mchod pa byas te/ phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces gsol to// sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi mchog/ de bzhin
9b2(rgyud): gshegs pa kun gyi gsang // bla na med pa'i byang chub sems// bcom ldan snying po bshad du gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku
9b3(rgyud): dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i bdag po'i/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsol ba btab pa mkhyen cing / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi sems kyi
9b4(rgyud): yong su rtog pa yang thugs kyis mkhyen nas/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// khyed kyis sems lus lta bu dang / lus sems lta bu dang /
9b5(rgyud): sems tshig tu brjod pa lta bur bskyed cig/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang /
9b6(rgyud): thugs na mkha' lta bur sbyar nas/ ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// e ma ho kun tu bzang po yis/ sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje can/ skye ba med pa'i tshul gyis su//
9b7(rgyud): skye ba 'di ni rab tu bsgrags/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa/ de bzhin gsheg
9b8(rgyud): po thams cad kyi mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i tshul rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsung so// dngos po med pas
10a1(rgyud): sgom pa med// bsgom par bya ba bsgom pa min// de ltar dngos po dngos med pas// bsgom pa dmig su med pa'o// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
10a2(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pas gsungaso// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis mngon par
10a3(rgyud): rtogs pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsung so// dngos po thams cad dang bral ba/ phung po khams dang skye mched dang //
10a4(rgyud): gzugs dang 'dzin pa rnams spangs pa// chos bdag med pa mnyam nyid pas/ rang sems bzod nas ma skyes pa// stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin no// zhes bcom ldan 'das
10a5(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyis gsung so// de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje mi bskyod pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mi zad pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i
10a6(rgyud): ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsung so// dngos po 'di rnams ma skyes pas// chos dang chos nyid med pa ste// na mkha' lta bur bdag
10a7(rgyud): med pas// byang chub tshul 'di brtan pa'o// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa mi bskyod pas gsungaso// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhi gshegs pa rin chen
10a8(rgyud): dpal de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyams par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsung sa/ chos rnams thams cad
10b1(rgyud): dngos med cing // chos kyi mtshan nyid rnam par spangs// bdag med chos la kun du byung // byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen dpal gyi
10b2(rgyud): gsungaso// // de nas bcom ldan 'das tshe dpag tu med pa 'od zer 'bar ba rdo rje sgron ma zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhags te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungaso
10b3(rgyud): ma skyes pa'i chos rnams la// ngo bo med de bsgom pa'ang med// na mkha'i gan su sbyor ba yis// de ltar dngos po rab tu bsgrags// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gsheg/
10b4(rgyud): pa tshe dpag tu med pas gsung so// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa grub pa gdon mi za ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa rdo rje
10b5(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungaso// chos rnams rang bzhin 'od gsal ba/ gdod nas dag pa na mkha' bzhin// byang chub
10b6(rgyud): med cing mngon rtogs med// byang chub tshul 'di bstan pa'o// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa grub pa gdon mi za bas gsung so// // de nas byams pa la sogs
10b7(rgyud): pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba'i chos de kho na nyid yi ge thos nas// /
10b8(rgyud): mtshar du myur rmad du gyur te/ ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// e ma ho sangs rgyas e me he chos/ chos bshad pa ni ngo mtshar che// yang dag don ni dag pa'i don// byang chub
11a1(rgyud): sems la phyag 'tshalo// bdag med pa'i chos las byung / sangs rgyas byang chub rdzogs mdzad pa// rnam par mi rtog mig su med// byang chub sems
11a2(rgyud): la phyag 'tshalo// kun tu bzang po thams cad don/ byang chub sems ni rab bskor ba// byang chub spyod pa rdo rje che/ byang chub sems la phyag 'tshalo// de bzhin gshegs pa'i
11a3(rgyud): thugs dag pa/ sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje 'dzin// sangs rgyas byang chub rab ston pa// byang chub sems la phyag 'tshalo// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung
11a4(rgyud): dang / thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa las// byang chub kyi sems kyi le'u ste// // gnyis pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
11a5(rgyud): thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'phro ba'i sprin bkod pa/ rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyom
11a6(rgyud): par zhugs te/ rdo rje bkod pa'i zhes bya bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u 'di gsung so// // oM shu n+ya ta gnya' na badz+ra swa b+ha ba ad ma ko haM/ na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gan
11a7(rgyud): par/ sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom pa ni/ 'od zer sprin gyi tshogs chen po// sangs rgyas 'bar ba'i 'od dang mnyam/ 'od zer sna lngas kun du khyab// kun nas yongasu
11a8(rgyud): zlum pa ste/ 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga yis khyab/ mchod pa rnam pa lngas brgyan pa// 'dor na de ltar bsgoms na su// gzugs ni dbusu bsgom par bya// rnam par snang mdzad bya/
11b1(rgyud): rgya che// sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan pa'o// sku gsung thugs ni rdo rje yi// phyag rgya 'am yang bsgom par bya/ tsho gas dang ni ldan pa yis// mi bskyod pa yi rgya mchog dang //
11b2(rgyud): dkon mchog dpal gyi rgya chen dang / tshe dpag med pa'i 'od byed dang // thobs med grub pa'i rgya chen rnams// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// sku gsung thug/
11b3(rgyud): kyi rdo rje can// in dra ni la'i kha dog 'dra// rab 'bar phyag na rdo rje bsnams// rnam par brtsigs la 'jigs 'jigs lha/ shel dang zla ba'i 'od 'dra ba// thor tshugs cod
11b4(rgyud): pan gyis brgyan pa/ rab 'bar phyag na 'khor lo bsnams// sna tshogs brgyan gyi mdzes par brgyan/ 'dzam bu'i chu bo'i gser 'od 'dra/ sangs rgyas sprin gyi kun du 'khrig/
11b5(rgyud): de yi phyag na rdo rje che/ rtse mo dgu par rnam par bsgom// ma ga ta yi 'od 'dra ba// rdo rje 'bar bas rnam par brgyan/ kun tu 'bar ba'i sprin gyi khyab/ phyag na rin chen bsnam
11b6(rgyud): par bsgom// pad ma ra gi mdog 'dra ba/ gtso bo 'dod chags 'bar ba mnga'// rab 'bar phyag na pad+ma bsnams/ 'dod chags rdo rje can bsgom bya// 'od zer sna lnga'i 'od
11b7(rgyud): 'dra'i sku/ gdon mi za ba rdo rje can// zhi ba phyag na ral dri rnams/ sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
11b8(rgyud): sku dang gsung dang / thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi dbyings ngo bo nyid rdo zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sku dang / gsung dang / thugs byin
12a1(rgyud): gyis brlob pa'i sngags 'di gsungaso// / oM d+harma d+ha du ad ma ko ha/ rin chen chen po kha dog lnga// yungs kar gyi ni 'bru tshad tsam/ sna yi rtse mor
12a2(rgyud): nan tan du// rnal 'byor pa yis rtag par bsgom/ rin chen brtan par gyur nas spro/ brtan pa ma gyur yong mi spro/ sangs rgyas 'bar ba 'dra ba'i 'od// mchog rab sprin
12a3(rgyud): rnams spro bar bya// 'khor lo rdo rje rin chen dang / pad+ma ral gri mtshon chen 'dzin// byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen rnams/ spro ba'i bdag nyid can gyis spro// na mkha'i
12a4(rgyud): dkyil gyi dbus gnas par/ rdo rje dkyil 'khor bri bar bya// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas pa/ 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ pad+ma'i dkyil
12a5(rgyud): 'khor 'dra ba ni/ zlas pa bsgom pas bsgom par bya// rin chen dkyil 'khor 'gro ba ni// rin chen brtson pas bsgom par bya// sbyin pa'i dkyil 'khor las byung ba// nam
12a6(rgyud): mkha' 'dra bar bri bar bya// 'di dag sangs rgyas rab kyi mchog/ sku gsung thugs ni bsgom pa yis/ dkyil 'khor rdo rje las byung ba// thams cad mkhyen pa'i tshul thob
12a7(rgyud): pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ rdo rje bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u ste/
12a8(rgyud): gsum pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin bzhin gshegs pa yang 'dus nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
12b1(rgyud): kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi bdag po la bstod pa'i rgyal po 'dis gsol ba btab bo// de bzhin gshegs pa kun zhi ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa kun gnas/
12b2(rgyud): chos kun bdag med pa'i mchog/ dkyil 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol// mtshan rnams thams cad yang dag rdzogs// mtshan min thams cad yang dag spangs// kun
12b3(rgyud): tu bzang po'i sku yi mchog/ dkyil 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol/ zhi ba'i chos ni mchog las byung // ye shes spyod pa rnam spong ba/ kun du bzang po gsung gi mchog/
12b4(rgyud): dkyil 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol/ sems can kun gyi sems chen po// rang bzhin dag cing dri ma med// kun bzang thugs mchog kha lo sgyur// dkyil 'khor/
12b5(rgyud): dam pa bshad du gsol// de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin/ 'jig rten gsum pa khams gsum pa/ 'jig rten gsum mchog rdo rje gtso// 'jig rten gsum mchog ston
12b6(rgyud): pa pos/ de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi thugs/ dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor rab 'dra ba/ dkyil 'khor rab tu nyams dga'
12b7(rgyud): bshad// de nas thugs kyi dkyil 'khor mchog/ thugs kyi rdo rje rab 'dra ba// sku dang gsung dang thugs rnams kyis// dkyil 'khor rab tu bshad par bya// lus ngag
12b8(rgyud): sems ni bsgom pa yis/ shes rab can gyi thig btab pa/ thig skud sar pa legs bkal/ tshad ma rab tu mdzes pa yis// shugs kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa de/ khru/
13a1(rgyud): ni bcu gnyis tshad du bya/ ngos bzhi dang ni grwa bzhir ldan/ sgo bzhi pa ni rab tu rtag/ de yi dbus su 'khor lo ni/ rab tu zlum po bri bar bya// de
13a2(rgyud): nas las kyi cho ga ni/ mthong bas phyag rgya dgod par bya// de dbus rdo rje bri ba ni/ in dra ni la'i kha dog 'dra/ 'bar bar ba chen po rtse lnga pa/ 'jigs pa dag kyang rab 'jig
13a3(rgyud): byed/ 'khor lo chen po shar phyogasu/ rdo rje 'bar bas rnam par brgyan/ rin chen chen po lho phyogasu// 'od zer mang po rab tu 'khrigs/ pad+ma chen po nub phyogasu// pad+ma ra ga
13a4(rgyud): kha dog 'dra/ ral gri chen po byang phyog su// 'od zer mang po rab tu 'khrigs// dbus na sprin dang 'dra ba'i 'od/ spyan ni shar gyi gra ru bri// ma ma ki ni rigs byung ba'i// rdo rje de
13a5(rgyud): bzhin lho phyogasu// pad+ma bye sdong bur bcas// nub phyogasu ni bri bar bya// ud pal mdzes pa byang phyogasu// mthing kha sprin dang 'dra bar bri/ tho ba 'bar ba 'od gsal ba// shar
13a6(rgyud): phyogs skor ni bri bar bya// rdo rje 'bar sogs 'od bzang ba// be con lho'i phyogasu bri// pad+ma 'bar ba 'od byed pa/ nub kyi phyogasu bri bar bya// rdo rje 'khyil pa rdo rje can// byang gi phyog
13a7(rgyud): su bri/ zugs kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa de/ yongasu gsal bar shes byas nas// lus dang ngag sems mchod pa yis// nan tan du ni mchod pa bya/ bud med rang
13a8(rgyud): tu med dngas gla/ lo drang bcu drug lon pa ni/ dri dang me tog phreng brgyan te/ yon tan ska rags ma ma kir/ shes rab can gyi byin rlabs la/ de'i dbus su mnyes pa/
13b1(rgyud): bya/ sangs rgyas zhi ba'i gnas spros pas// na mkha'i dbyings ni rab tu brgyan// bshang lci khu ba khrag la sogs// lha rnams la ni dbul bar bya// de ltar byas na sa
13b2(rgyud): rgyas dang // byang chub sems dpa' grags chen mnyis// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'das pa
13b3(rgyud): pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor gyi le'u ste bzhi pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa ni/ kun gyi sku dang gsung thugs kyi
13b4(rgyud): rdo rje 'chang gi rgyal po ni/ gnas kyi dbang phyug kun mchog gi/ spyod pa kun mchog chos kyi don/ spyod pa'i mtshan nyid bka' stsal to// rnam par mi rtog don las byung
13b5(rgyud): 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug rigs// theg pa'i mchog ni bla med pa'i/ dngos grub rab mchog bsgrub par byed// rigs ngan smig ma mkhan la sogs// gsod don
13b6(rgyud): don gnyer sems pa rA p+paSha dang / theg chen bla na med pa yi// theg mchog 'di las 'grub par 'gyur/ sems can mtshams med la sogs pa'i// sdig pa chen po
13b7(rgyud): byed pa yang // rdo rje theg pa rgya mtsho de/ theg pa mchog ni 'di la 'grub// snying nas slob dpon smod pa dag/ bsgrub kyang 'grub par long mi 'gyur/ srog gcod
13b8(rgyud): pa'i sems can gang // bdun du sla ba dga' ba dang / gzhan gyi nor ma chags pa dang / 'jug tu 'ad pa spyang gang dang // gshang kyi bsul ba'o// de dag 'asgra
14a1(rgyud): pa'i snod du gyur/ ma dang sring mo bu mo la/ 'dod pa bas ni mnyes byas na/ theg chen mchog gi chos nyid kyi// dngos grub rgya chen de 'azho
14a2(rgyud): bo/ sangs rgyas gtso bos yul dag la// rnam par mi rtog blo can gyi// mnyes par byas kyang mi gos te/ de ni sangs rgyas 'grub par 'gyur// de nas sgrib pa
14a3(rgyud): thams cad rnam par sel ba la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams/ ngo mtshar du gyur// rmad du gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin ga
14a4(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi bdag po ci'i slad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi nang du 'di lta bu'i tshig ngan pa gsung zhes gsol to// de nas de bzhin gshegs
14a5(rgyud): ba thams cad kyis/ sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel bas la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi tshig gsan nas/ byang chub sems
14a6(rgyud): dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu rnams mthong / de skad ma zer cig/ ye shes snying po can rnams kyis// sangs rgyas chos nyid dag/
14a7(rgyud): pa 'di/ snying po chos kyi don las byung // byang chub spyod pa'i gnas 'di yin// de nas yang brjod kyis mi lang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing phra rab la sogs pa'i rdul phra mo/
14a8(rgyud): snyed kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ 'jigs skrag nas rgyal bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis/ byang chub sems dpa
14b1(rgyud): de dag rgyal bar gyur pa gzigs nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi bdag po la 'di skad ces gsol to//
14b2(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa'i sems dpa' chen po 'di dag bslang bar gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang /
14b3(rgyud): gsung dang / thugs rdo rje/ de bzhin gshegs pas na mkha' dang mnye pa'i gnyis mu med pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhug so// snyoms
14b4(rgyud): par zhugs ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i bdag po'i/ 'od kyi reg pa tsam gyis de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po
14b5(rgyud): de dag rang rang gi stan la gnas par gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ngo mtshar du gyur// rmad du gyur/ dges pas khyab par gyur nas/ chos
14b6(rgyud): kyi dbyangs 'di skad ces gsungaso// e ma'o e ma'o chos/ e ma'o chos kyi don byung ba/ chos don dag pa bdag med pas// rdo rje rgyal po phyag 'tshal 'dud/
14b7(rgyud): skra dang gsung thugs rab tu dag/ 6// nam mkha' dang ni mnyam nyid nas// rnam par mi 'gyur snang ba med// rdo rje sku la phyag 'tshal 'dud// thugs ni de bzhin
14b8(rgyud): gshegs pa'i gtso// dus gsum dag gi lam du byung / na mkha' chen po'i dbyings gyur pa// na mkha' lam la phyag 'tshal 'dud// namakha'i sku las yang
15a1(rgyud): / dag byung // na mkha'i lam la gnas pa po// na mkha'i thugs ni chos kyi mchog/ spyod pa'i gnas la phyag 'tshalo// de bzhin gshegs pa
15a2(rgyud): thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las kun tu spyod pa'i mchog gi le'u ste// / lnga pa'o// // de nas de
15a3(rgyud): bzhin gshegs rdo rje mi bskyod pa// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhags
15a4(rgyud): te thugs byin gyis brlab pa'i sngags 'di gsung so// os pa ta thrig ta 'adz+ras b+hA ba yang ma ka hA/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rjenas
15a5(rgyud): par snang mdzad rdul dang bral ba'i gnas rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sku byin gyis brlab pa'i sngags 'di gsung so/ oM sarba ta thAg tu/
15a6(rgyud): ka ya badz+ra swa b+ha ba ad ma ko haM/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag tu med pa mnyam pa nyid mi dmigs pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la
15a7(rgyud): snyoms par zhugs te/ gsung byin gyis brlab pa'i sngags 'di gsungaso/ oM sarba ta thA ga ta tha ka badz+ra swa b+hA ba ad ma ko hang // rdo rje gsum po de bzhin ga
15a8(rgyud): pa'i gsang / gnas ni gnas kyi rnam par bsgom par bya/ sngags kyi mtshan gyi shin du mtshan byas la// mchog rab 'di yis bsgrub pa nyid du bya// de nas bcom ldan
15b1(rgyud): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dkon mchog dpal ye shes sgron ma zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sngags 'di gsungaso// oM sarba ta thA ga ta a
15b2(rgyud): nur ga badz+ra swa b+ha ba ad ma ko haM// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa grub pa rdo rje gdon mi za ba/ rdo rje gdon mi za ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyom
15b3(rgyud): bzhugs te/ sngags 'di gsungaso// oM sarba ta thA ga ta pu tsa badz+ra swa b+ha wa ad ma ko haM/ rtag tu 'dod pa'i yon tan lngas/ sangs tshul bzhin mchod par bya/ mchod pa rna
15b4(rgyud): pa lnga rnas kyi/ myur du sangs nyid thob 'gyur/ zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs kyi bdag po rdo rje 'chang bas
15b5(rgyud): gsungaso// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs kyi bdag po po rdo rje 'dzin gyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
15b6(rgyud): sngags kyi gsang ba 'di gsungaso// sngags la dmigs pa'i lus dang ni/ ngag dang yid kyis bskul na su// yid ni dga' zhing mgu ba yis// dngos grub rab mchog bsgrub
15b7(rgyud): bar bya/ sems la dmigs byas bdag med pas/ ngag dang lus kyang rnam par bsgom// na mkha' bzhin du mnyam pa'i gnas/ sbyor ba rnam gsum bsgrub par bya//
15b8(rgyud): lus dang ngags dang sems dmigs na/ ngo bo nyid ni dmigasu med/ sngags kyi lus su sbyor ba la/ byang chub med cing sgom pa med/ sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan nyid
16a1(rgyud): du/ 'di ni mdor nanam spyad nas/ sngags kyi brtag pa'i ting nge 'dzin/ byang chub sbyor ba bsgom par bya// de nas dpal ldan rdo 'dzin/ de bzhin
16a2(rgyud): gshegs kun gyi mchod/ sangs rgyas kun mchog kun mkhyen gyis/ bsgom pa'i mchog ni bka' stsal to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// zla ba'i dkyil 'kho
16a3(rgyud): bsgom par bya/ sangs rgyas gas ni rab bsgom nas/ phra mo'i sbyor ba kun tu brtsam// sna'i rtse mo yung kar bsam// 'gro dang mi 'gro yungs kar la/ ye shes gnas ni
16a4(rgyud): nyams dga' ba/ gsang ba'i ye shes kyis brtags bsgom// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ sangs sku'i gnas
16a5(rgyud): bsgoms te/ de'i steng du gnas bzhag go// hUM na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ spyan gyi tshul du sbyor ba la// rdo rje
16a6(rgyud): pad+ma rnam par bsgom// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ rin chen dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ dang po'i sbyor ba nan tan gyis// de'i stengs du yongasu bsgom//
16a7(rgyud): nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ pad+ma'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ gsung gi rdo rje tshul sbyor bas// 'dod chags rdo rje spyan bsgom bya// na mkha'i dpying
16a8(rgyud): kyi dbus gnas par/ 'od kyi dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ sangs rgyas tshul ni zhi ba sgo/ 'khor dang khyad par dag tu spro/ ud pal thing ka'i mdog 'dra ba
16b1(rgyud): rtse mo lnga pa khyad par da/ bsgo kyi 'bru tsam nan tan gyi// sna'i rtse mor rnam par bsam/ tsa na ka'i 'bru tsam la// 'dam brgyad pa ge ser bcas// sna'i rtse mor 'di
16b2(rgyud): shes te/ bsgom pas byang chub gzhol bar 'gyur/ 'khor lo la sogs khyed par da// bsgom pa der ni brtag par bya/ dngos grub thams yon tan gnas// nyams
16b3(rgyud): dga' byang chub gnas 'grub 'gyur/ sangs rgyas byang chub gnas rnams ni/ de ru 'dor na spro bar bya// sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan ma yis// chos kyi tshig rnam rab
16b4(rgyud): tu brjod/ de nas dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin/ de nyid don kun ston pa pos// spyod pa kun mchog legs dag pa// gsang sngags dam pa bka' stsal to// gzug
16b5(rgyud): dang sgra dang ro ldan par/ she rab can gyi zla drug bsgom// gsang de nyid mchod sbyin gyi// legs par mchod nas bsgom par bya// dngos grub 'bras bu 'dod pa yi
16b6(rgyud): zas su gshang lce zos nas ni/ sangs rgyas byang chub skyon med pa// yang dag bla med 'grub par 'gyur// za su sha rnams za ba dang // sha chen rnams ni rab rtags na// /
16b7(rgyud): sku dang gsung dang thugs gsang ba'i/ dngos grub thams cad 'grub par 'gyur/ glang po'i sha dang rta'i sha// de bzhin dam pa khyi'i sha// zas kyi phyir ni za' bar
16b8(rgyud): bye/ zas gzhan dag ni ma zos na// byang chub sems dpa' blo can dang / sangs rgyas rnams ni mnyes par 'gyur/ 'di lta bu yi sbyor ba yis// myur du sangs
17a1(rgyud): rgyas nyid thob 'gyur/ 'dod khams dbang phyug 'jig rten na/ go 'phang las ni 'jig par 'gyur// gtso bo gzi can stobs dang ldan//
17a2(rgyud): mdangs bzang mthong na yid du 'ong / mthong ba tsam gyis bskul ba yis// 'jig rten 'di dag dbang du 'gyur/ 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ gsang ba byang
17a3(rgyud): chub dam pa ste/ yang dag sngags kyi gsang ba 'di// lus ngag sems las 'das pa'o// / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs kyi
17a4(rgyud): gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ sku dang / gsung dang / thugs byin gyis brlob pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
17a5(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi bdag pos dam tshig chen po'i de kho na nyid sngags spyod pa'i mchog/ mngon par rdzogs par byang /
17a6(rgyud): chub pa'i le'u 'di gsung so// // 'dod pa'i long spyod thams cad la/ ji ltar 'dod pa rten na ni// 'di lta bu'i sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas myur du thob par 'gyur/
17a7(rgyud): 'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad ni/ ji ltar 'dod pa rten byas te// rang gi lha'i sbyor ba yis// bdag dang gzhan la mchod par bya// dka' thub sdom pa mi zad pas/
17a8(rgyud): brtan kyang 'grub par mi 'gyur gyi/ 'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad la// brten kyang myur du 'grub par 'gyur// slong mo za zhing mi bzlas te/ slong ma'ang dga' bar
17b1(rgyud): mi bya'o// 'dod pa kun la longs spyod cing // sngags kyi yan lag ma nyams bzlas// lus dang ngags dang sems rnams ni// bde bar gnas na byang chub thob//
17b2(rgyud): gzhan du dus min 'chi ba dang // dmyal bar nges par bsreg par 'gyur/ sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' dang // sngags kyi spyod pa mchog spyod rnams// /
17b3(rgyud): chos mchog mi g.yo brnyes pa yang // 'dod pa thams cad brtan paso// chags can ye shes 'dod pa yis// rtag tu 'dod yon lnga rnams brtem/ byang chub
17b4(rgyud): sems dpa' skyes par bya// byang chub nyi ma chags par bya// gzugs rnams gsum shes byas nas// mchod pa byed pas mchod par bya// de nyid bcom ldan sna
17b5(rgyud): tshogs pa// sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad gzhi/ sgra pa rnam gsum shes byas nas// lha rnams la ni dbul bar bya// de nyid bcom ldan sna tshogs pa//
17b6(rgyud): sangs rgyas rin chen 'byung gnas gtso// dri la rnam gsum shes byas nas/ sangs rgyas tshogs la dbul bar bya// de nyid bcom ldan sna tshogs pa// 'dod
17b7(rgyud): chags chos kyi 'byung gnas gtso// ro la rnam gsum shes byas nas/ lha rnams la ni dbul bar bya// de nyid sangs rgyas sna tshogs// sangs rgyas thog med rje
17b8(rgyud): 'dzin/ reg pa rnam gsum shes byas// bdag gi rigs la dbul bar bya/ de nyid bcom ldan rdo rje can/ mi bskyed pa'i tshul brnyes pa'o// gzugs sgra rol
18a1(rgyud): sogs pa la/ rtag tu sems ni sbyar bar bya/ 'di de sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ gsang ba'i snying po btus pa'o// gzugs sgra dri sron
18a2(rgyud): sngags pa yi/ lha nyid du ni rtag tu bsgom/ yang na de la bsgom pa ni/ rigs kyi tshul du rnam par bsgom// sangs rgyas rjesu dran pa sbyor// chos ni rje su dran bsgo
18a3(rgyud): sku dang gsung dang thugs rnams bsgom// rdo rje su dran bsgom pa/ rigs ni rjesu dran par sbyor/ khro bo rje su dran bsgom pa/ lha ni rje su dran par sbyor// bsgom
18a4(rgyud): byang chub thob par 'gyur/ bud med gzugs bzang mdangs bzang ba/ lo grang bcu drug lon pa la/ byin gyis brlabs kyis gnas gsum gyis// dben par
18a5(rgyud): mchod pa rab tu brtsam/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i btsun mo mchog/ spyan la sogs pa sgom par bya/ dbang po gnyis ni mnyam sbyar bas/ sangs rgyas dngos
18a6(rgyud): grub thob par 'gyur/ yi ge hUM dang oM dag dang / phaT kyang rab tu bsgom par bya// 'od zer sna lngas khyab pa yi// pad+mo rdo rje bsgom par bya// 'bar bcas zla 'od bzhin
18a7(rgyud): du dkar/ yid du 'ong ba bsgom par bya/ sangs rgyas rjes dran sbyor la sogs// byang chub 'dod pas bsgom par bya/ de la sangs rgyas rjesu dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe
18a8(rgyud): na// b+ha ga la ni ling ka bzhag/ sangs rgyas gzugs ni bsgom par bya/ ba spu rnams kyi bu ga nas// mkhas pas sangs rgyas sprin rnams spro// de la chos rjesu dran pa
18b1(rgyud): ji ltar bsgom zhe na// b+ha ga la ni ling ka bzhag/ rdo rje'i chos ni bsgom par bya/ ba spu rnams kyi bu ga nas// mkhas pas chos kyi sprin rnams spro// de la rdo rje rjes
18b2(rgyud): dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na// b+ha ga la ni ling ka bzhag/ rdo rje sems dpa' rnam par bsgom/ ba spu rnams kyi bu ga nas// rdo rje'i sprin rnams spro bar bya// de la
18b3(rgyud): rigs rjesu dran par ji ltar bsgom zhe na/ b+ha ga la ni ling ka bzhag/ sangs rgyas gzugs ni rab tu bsgom// ba spu rnams kyi bu ga nas// mkhas pas rigs kyi sprin
18b4(rgyud): rnams spro// de la khro bo rjes su dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na// b+ha ga la ni ling ka bzhag/ khro bo dbang po rab tu bsgom// ba spu rnams kyi bu ga nas/ mkhas pas khro
18b5(rgyud): bos sprin rnams spro// de la dam tshig rje su dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na/ bdag gi rdo rje pad+mar ldan// dbang po gnyis ni mnyam sbyar te// rang gi khu ba'i thigs pa
18b6(rgyud): yis/ sangs rgyas rdo rje sems dpa' mchod/ de la dkyil 'khor rjesu dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na/ dbang po gnyis ni mnyam sbyar te// mkhas pas rang gi
18b7(rgyud): bdag/ rnal 'byor pas ni rtag tu 'byung // dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor tshul du bya/ de la sku rjesu dran pa ji lta bsgom zhe na/ sangs rgyas kun gyi sku gang yin//
18b8(rgyud): phung po kun gyi rab tu rgyas/ sang+yas sku yi rang bzhin gyis// bdag kyang de dang 'drar gyur cig/ de la gsung rje su dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na// rdo rje chos kyi gsum
19a1(rgyud): gang yin// gsung des nges tshig phun sum tshogs// bdag gi tshig kying de 'dra ste/ chos 'dzin pa dang 'dra gyur cig/ de la thugs rjesu dran
19a2(rgyud): pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na/ gsang ba'i bdag po blo ldan pa/ kun tu bzang po thugs gang yin/ rdo rje 'dzin pa lta bur ni// bdag gi sems kyang de 'drar 'gyur//
19a3(rgyud): de la sems rjesu dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na/ sems can kun gyi sems gang yin/ sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi mtshan// de ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/
19a4(rgyud): mkha' dang mtshungs par spyod gyur cig/ de la sngags thams cad kyi gzugs dang / sku dang gsung dang thugs rjesu dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na// sngags kyi rdo
19a5(rgyud): rje'i sku gang yin// gsung gi sku yang rnams bsgom pa// bdag kyang rtag tu de 'dra bar/ sngags 'dzin pa dang mnya ma gyur cig/ de la dam tshig rje su dran pa ji ltar
19a6(rgyud): bsgom zhe na// khu ba phyung ste cho ga bzhin// 'bras bu 'dod pas btung bar bya// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs bsang na/ dngos grub rab tu thob par 'gyur/ de la
19a7(rgyud): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i rjesu dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na/ rang bzhin gyis ni 'od gsal ba// thams cad ma skyes zag pa med// byang chub med cing mngon rtog
19a8(rgyud): med// khams kyang med cing 'byung ba'ang med// de la ma skyes pa rjesu dran pa ji ltar bsgom zhe na// thams cad rang bzhin 'od gsal ba// mtshan med mi 'gyur
19b1(rgyud): nam mkha' bzhin// gnyis med gnyi su med min// shin du dri med na mkha' bzhin// / de la zhe sdang gi rigs la sogs pa'i mchod pa rje su dran pa ji ltar/
19b2(rgyud): bsgom zhe na/ bud med sems ni rab brtan pa/ lo grangs bcu gnyis lon rnyed la// rigs kyi sbyor bas rab bsgom te// bdag gi khu bas mchod par bya//
19b3(rgyud): 'dis ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku// rdo rje 'dzin pa'i thugs dang ni/ chos 'dzin mchog gi gsung dag kyang // tshe 'di nyid la thob par 'gyur/ sku dang gsung
19b4(rgyud): dang thugs kyang 'grub// gang gzhan phra mor bshad pa'i rnams// rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms te// zlas pa tsam gyi de 'grub 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa than
19b5(rgyud): cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ sngags kyi spyod pa'i mchog gi le'u ste// / bdun pa'o//
19b6(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje dkon mchog dpal gyis// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po// dbang phyug/
19b7(rgyud): dam pa rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po la bstod pa 'dis gsol ba btab po// / rdo rje sems dpa' theg pa che/ na mkha'i spyod pa rnams sbyong ba// kun tu bzang po
19b8(rgyud): spyod pa'i mchog/ rgyal mchog mchod pa bshad du gsol// 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug che// rdo rje theg par rab ston pa/ nam kho'i dbyings dang mtshungs/
20a1(rgyud): pa'i mchog/ rgyal gzhi mchod pa bshad du gsol/ thar pa'i lam ni rab ston pa/ theg pa gsum gyi lam na gnas// sangs rgyas skal
20a2(rgyud): mchog dag pa'i bdag/ mi mchod mchod pa bshad du gsol// byang chub ses ni rgyas pa'i spyan// chos kyi 'khor lo rab bskor ba/ sku dang gsung thugs shin
20a3(rgyud): du dag/ phyag 'tshal rdo rje la theg pa la'o// // de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// thams cad na mkha' mi 'gyur che/ thams cad dbang bskur kun gyi don// kun
20a4(rgyud): dbang rdo rje rin chen 'dzin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod pa'i mchog/ rdo rje mi phyed gsum gnas pa/ sku dang gsung dang thugs bskal mchog/ rgyal ba 'byung
20a5(rgyud): ba 'gyur bar bshad// na chung gzhon nu mig yangs pa// gzugs bzang gzhon pas brgyan pa ni// lo grangs nyi shu lnga lon snyed// byol song las kyang rab tu
20a6(rgyud): brtag/ sa phyogs gtsang zhing rnam par dben pa'am// rgya nyid skyes zhi zhi ba'i gnas rnamasu/ gshang lci chu la sogs pa byug pa 'am/ rgyal ba mchod phyir rtag
20a7(rgyud): par rab tu bya/ nu ma'i dbus par spyi gtsug mtha' bar/ chog shes pas yang na rkang pa'i bar/ lte ba rked pa gsang ba'i rgyal ba'i sras/ rigs lnga rnams
20a8(rgyud): ni dgod par rab tu bya/ na mkha'i dbyangs kyi dbus gnas par/ ye shes rgya mtsho bsgom par bya/ bdag nyid zla ba'i dbus gnas par/ mkhas pas
20b1(rgyud): snying khar bsgom par bya// zhi ba rdo rje 'dzin 'dod na/ bsdu ba dag kyang rab tu bya/ rin chen sna bzhi'i mchod rten la// 'od zer 'phreng bas rnam par brgyan/
20b2(rgyud): ye shes rgya mtsho dus gsum du/ gnas de yin pa rnam par bsam// bdag gi ba spu'i bu ga nas// mkhas pas mchod pa'i sprin rnams spro/ mkhas pas
20b3(rgyud): ud pa la dag dang / pad+ma rnam pa lnga zhes bya/ dza ti rnams gsum shes byas nas/ lha rnams la ni dbul bar bya// me tog kar ni ka ra dang // ma ti ka dang
20b4(rgyud): yu ti ka// me tog ka ra bi rar bsam/ mchod pa thams cad rab tu brtag/ dpag tshad rgya'i khyon tsam du/ 'khor lo dkyil 'khor bsgom byas la//
20b5(rgyud): rnam par mkhas pas rtag pA ni/ rigs rnams rab tu dgod par bya/ de bzhin pad+mo rdo rje dang // ral gri ud pa la mkhas pas bsgom// dpag tshad bye bI
20b6(rgyud): khyon tsam la// gru bzhi shin du mdzes pa yi// mchod rten rin chen sna bzhi pa/ gsal zhing rang bzhin dri ma med// rigs rnams thams cad mchod pa'i phyir
20b7(rgyud): shes rab can gyi gnas bsgom// 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga rnams kyis// de la mchod pa rgya mtsho brtsam// rin chen na bza' la sogs pas// byang chub 'don
20b8(rgyud): pas rtag tu mchod/ mchod pa rnams lnga'i mchog rnams kyis// rtag tu lha rnams mnyes par bya// rin chen 'byung gnas na chungs mchog rin chen sna tshogs
21a1(rgyud): mchog gi brgyan// bsgrub tshe rab tu 'grub pa'i phyir// sangs rgyas kun la dbul bar bya/ zhing 'dir rin chen sna bdun gyis// mkhas pa
21a2(rgyud): dag gi yongs kang la/ dngos grub 'dod pas sbyin pa'i phyir// nyin re shes rab can gyis dbul/ bdag po'i phyag rgyar mnyam bzhag la// sangs rgyas
21a3(rgyud): dkyil 'khor dbus dag tu// 'dod chags blo can sangs rgyas la// re ba'i sbyor ba dbul bar bya// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ dkyil 'khor
21a4(rgyud): bkod pa bsgom par bya/ de bzhin gshegs pa bdag gi lus// bla ma bshang dang gci bas mchod/ bzhin bzang shin tu mdzes pa yis// na chung bskal pa mchog
21a5(rgyud): ldan pa// byin gyis brlabs kyis gnas bsams te/ sangs rgyas mchod pa rab tu brtag/ mig bzang brtan pa'i blo ldan pas// khu ba blang nas bza' bar bya/
21a6(rgyud): 'di ni sngags rnams thams cad kyi// sku gsung thugs kyi mchod pa ste/ ye shes rdo rje can gyi gsang // sngags rnams dngos grub byed par gsungs//
21a7(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang // gsung dang thugs kyi gsangag gsang ba 'dus pa las/ gshang lci dam tshig gi le'u s+ho// brgyad pa'o//
21a8(rgyud): / de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin/ thams cad na mkha'i mi 'gyur che// thams cad dbang bskur spyod pa'i mchog/ dbang phyug dam pa kun don gyis// sku
21b1(rgyud): gsung thugs la longs spyod pa// rdo rje mi phyed gsum dkyil 'khor// sangs rgyas ye shes spyan gyi sang // nyam dga' mchog ni rab tu bshad// na mkha'
21b2(rgyud): dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// rdo rje mi bskyod rab bsgom nas// lag tu rdo rje bsgom par bya// 'od 'phro mang ba
21b3(rgyud): 'bar ba dang // 'od zer sna lngas rab tu gang // dus gsum pa'i sangs rgyas rnams/ bsgoms nas rdo rje phye mar klag/ sku gsung thugs kyi long spyod
21b4(rgyud): ni// rdo rje cher klag med gyur pa// bsam gtan mchog ni bsgom na ni// thugs kyi dngos grub thob par 'gyur/ rdo rje gsang ba 'di lta bus// sems
21b5(rgyud): can thams cad gsad na ni/ mi bskyod sangs rgyas zhing dag tu// rgyal ba'i sra su skye bar 'gyur/ 'di ni zhe sdang rigs kyi dam tshig gi de kho na ste//
21b6(rgyud): rigs thams cad kyi rgya mtsho yin par shes par bya'o// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin/ ye shes thar pa rab bsgrub pa/ ngo bo nyid dag dgos pa med//
21b7(rgyud): byang chub spong pa rab ston pas// sangs rgyas byang chub bsgrub pa yi/ yang dag dam tshig bka' stsal to// na mkha' dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ 'dra
21b8(rgyud): me'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ rnam par snang mdzad rab bsgoms te// sangs rgyas thams cad rnam par bsgom// rin chen kun gyi sbyor ba'i/
22a1(rgyud): / rdo rje'i gzugs ni rab tu brtag/ nor rnams thams cad phrogs na su// rdo rje gsum du rnams bsgo na/ nor gyi rgya mtshos gang ba yi//
22a2(rgyud): yid bzhin nor bu 'dra bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun gyi sras rnams dang / thub pa'i skyes bu mchog tu 'gyur/ 'di ni rigs kyi rgya mtsho thams cad las/
22a3(rgyud): gti mug gi rigs kyi dam tshig yang dag pa nyid du shes par bya'o// / de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin/ 'dod chags thar pa rab bsgrub par// gas
22a4(rgyud): dag pa dmigs med pa'i// dkyir 'khor rab tu bka' stsal to// nam mkha' dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ pad+ma'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ dpag med
22a5(rgyud): tshe ni rab bsgoms te/ sangs rgyas rnams kyi thams cad gang / bud med lta bur sbyar ba ni/ dam tshig gzhi yi sbyor ba yis// 'di ni rdo rje tshul mchog go// dpa
22a6(rgyud): po gnyis ni rab sbyor bas/ de dag thams cad nye bar spyad/ 'di ni rdo rje thams cad kyi// mi phyed sku gsum bsgom pa'o// 'di ni 'dod chags kyi yang dag
22a7(rgyud): pa'i dam tshig ste/ sngags pa rnams kyi sgom par bya'o// // de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje sngags kyi don bsgrub pa/ bdag med ye shes las byung ba
22a8(rgyud): gsung ni 'di skad bka' stsal to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ rdo rje thog med rab bsgom te// sangs
22a9(rgyud): thams cad de ru bsgom par byad
22b1(rgyud): rgyas thams cad bsgom par bya// thams cad gzugasu rnams bsgoms nas// rdo rje tshig gi brdzun smra bas// rgyal ba kun gyi gnas rnams dang // rgyal ba thams
22b2(rgyud): cad bslu bar bya// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ na mkha'i gsung ste dri ma med/ ye shes blo can kun gyi gsang // sngags kyi dngos grub thob par bshad// 'di
22b3(rgyud): ni dam tshig 'gugs pa'i rigs kyi dam tshig gi kho na nyid de/ don ji lta ba bzhin du spro bar bya'o// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin/ rdo rje mi phyed gsum rgyal gnas// rdo
22b4(rgyud): rje dngos grub rab ston pa// gsung ni 'di skad bka' stsal to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ dam tshig dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ dkon mchog
22b5(rgyud): dpal ni rab bsgom te/ gzugs rnams kun gyi 'di dag gang // btsub pa'i ngag la sogs pa ni/ brten na ye shes thob par 'gyur// // bcom ldan 'das
22b6(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje bkod pas de skad ces bka' stsal to// de nas yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig rdo rje dpal la sog
22b7(rgyud): pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ngo mtshar du gyur cing // rmad du gyur nas rdo rje'i tshig 'di smra so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa zam
22b8(rgyud): cad kyi bdag po/ khams gsum las 'das shing / 'jig rten thams cad las 'das pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'
23a1(rgyud): thams cad kyi 'khor gyi nang du/ 'di lta bu'i yang dag pa ma yin pa'i tshig gi lam rdo rje'i tshig 'di ci'i slad du gsung / de nas bcom
23a2(rgyud): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis mi lang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi ri rab kyi rdul phra mo snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig
23a3(rgyud): gi rdo rje dpal la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu sman pa'i 'du shes dang / smad pa'i 'du shes 'di
23a4(rgyud): lta bu ma bskyed cig/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste// sngags kyi spyod pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod pa'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ nam
23a5(rgyud): mkha' ni thams cad kyis rjesu song ba ste/ chos thams cad kyang na mkha'i khongasu btogs pa'o// chos de dag thams cad kyang 'dod pa'i khams na mi gnas//
23a6(rgyud): gzugs kyi khams ni mi gnas/ gzugs med pa'i khams na mi gnas/ 'byung ba chen po bzhi la yang mi gan so// rigs kyi bu chos thams cad kyang de ltar
23a7(rgyud): rje su rig par bya'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ni don dbang 'di lta bu mkhyen cing / sems can rnams kyi bsam pa mkhyen nas chos 'chad par mdzad//
23a8(rgyud): rigs kyi bu de ltar na mkha'i tshig nges par brjod pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dam tshig de dag rje su rig par bya'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na/ brtsub
23b1(rgyud): shing dang / brtsub brtan dang / mi'i lag pa skyod pa'i dbang gis/ du ba myur du 'byung zhing / me 'byung bar 'gyur mod kyi/ de yang brtsub shing la mi gnas/
23b2(rgyud): rtsub brtan la yang mi gnas/ ma'i lag pa bskyod pa la yang mi gan so// rigs kyi bu de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i dam tshig
23b3(rgyud): 'gro ba dang / 'ong ba la sogs pas rjesu rig par bya'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag ngo mtshar du gyur/ rmad du gyur/ rngam shing mig gdangs te/ tshig
23b4(rgyud): 'di skad ces smra'o// rmad byung chen po'i rna chos rnams ni/ na mkha' dang ni tshungs pa dang // rnam par mi rtog dag pa la// kun rdzob du yang bshad pa mtshar//
23b5(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi skra dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ don dam pa'i dag pa ste kho na nyid kyi don gyi/
23b6(rgyud): dam tshig gi le'u ste// dgu pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang 'dus te// bcom ldan 'das
23b7(rgyud): dam tshig chen po'i rdo rje de kho na nyid mngon par rdzogs par byang chub par/ sku dang / gsung dang / thugs gsang ba de bzhin gshegs pa la phyag 'tshal te/
23b8(rgyud): 'di skad ces gsol to// de nyid sngags snying kun btus pa/ sku dang gsung thugs gsang bar bsgrags// ngos grub chen po'i tshul gyi mchog/ yang dag bcom ldan
24a1(rgyud): bshad du gsol// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin/ nyon mongs kun gyi rgya mtsho gtso// 'bar ba drag po spyan yang pas// gsung ni 'di skad bka' stsal
24a2(rgyud): to// lus dang ngag dang yid rnams ni// rnam par mi rtog mi dmigs pa/ gang la'ang mi gnas mnyam pa nyid/ sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje bsgom// de nas bcom 'das de
24a3(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dag pa/ pha rol tu phyin pa sngags kyi tshul rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa de dag
24a4(rgyud): thams cad la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thos cad mi bskyod pa la sogs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
24a5(rgyud): rig pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma dang thabs gcig tu sems can thams cad kyi don bya ba la rol pa ston par mdzad de/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams mthas
24a6(rgyud): klas par 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga rnams kyis rol cing dgyes par yongasu spyod pa yod kyang // de dag sngags spyod pa la mngon par brtson pa rnams la/ kye ma 'di
24a7(rgyud): dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sngags kyi spyod pa'i tshul gyi chos rdzogs par gyur to// snyam nas/ spyan ras kyis mi 'tsho ste/ de bas na skyes bu dam
24a8(rgyud): pa de rnams la spyan ras kyis btsa' ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i sngags kyi gsang ga gsang ba thams cad
24b1(rgyud): kyi snying po kun tu bskul bar byed pa zhes bya ba rab tu gsang ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi dam tshig la dmig
24b2(rgyud): pa rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi dam tshig la dmigs pa chos 'dzin pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs kyi dam
24b3(rgyud): tshig gi lam nges par brjod pas/ sngags bsdus pa 'di lta bu gsungaso// hUM oM a swA hA// de nas 'di ni gsungs tsam gyi// sangs rgyas sras dang bcas pa
24b4(rgyud): kun// rab tu 'dar zhing rgyal bar 'gyur// rdo rje sems dpa' rje su dran// de nas phyag na rdo rjes de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gdag po'i dam tshig 'di
24b5(rgyud): gsungaso// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// bkod pa'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ de'i dbus nas yi ge hUM/ rang gi gzugasu rab tu brtag/ rdo rje
24b6(rgyud): 'od zer cher 'bar ba// rnam par 'phro bar bsam par bya/ sangs rgyas kyi ni sku gsung thugs/ drangs par de yis rnams bsgom na// de ma thag tu der
24b7(rgyud): 'gyur bar// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje sems dpa' rgyal po che// kun gyi gtso bo dbang phyug mchog/ rang gi dkyil 'khor rang rdo rjes// bskyed
24b8(rgyud): par byed pa'i tshul du 'gyur/ 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ snying po rdo rje bsdus pa yin// rang sngags skyes bu bsgom nas ni/ gnas bzhi rnamasu gzug
25a1(rgyud): kyi tshul// zhal gsum lta bu'i sbyor ba yis// kha dog gsum du rab tu bsgom// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje dam tshig gi de skad ces bka' stsal
25a2(rgyud): to// de la 'di ni rdo rje mchog gi gsang ba'o// snying kho'i dbus kyi phra mo yi/ dkyil 'khor rnams ni bsam par bya/ yi ge mchog tu gyur pa'i tshig/ de'i dbus
25a3(rgyud): bsam par bya// rdo rje chen po rtse lnga pa/ rtag tu sbyor ba bsgom par bya// rdo rje skyo ba'i sbyor ba yis// rdo rje gsum rnams bsgom par bya// de'i snying khar brdab byas
25a4(rgyud): te/ lha rnams rab tu bskul bar bya/ 'di ni rdo rje thams cad kyi/ sangs rgyas byang chub rab bsgrub pa'o// rdo rje pad+mo'i rigs la sogs// rdo rje kyo ba rnams bsgo zhing /
25a5(rgyud): snying kha ru ni bskul bar bshad/ 'di ni rol mo'i 'byung ba ste// rdo rje yi ni tshul mchog 'di// zhag bdun bar du byas nas ni/ ye shes rdo rje can gyi gsang // sku dang
25a6(rgyud): gsung thugs 'grub par 'gyur// mchog 'tshol pa dag rnam par gzigs// yid ni 'jig shing skra gyur nas// yid la 'gu zhing dga' gyur pa'i// dngos grub
25a7(rgyud): rgya chen ster byar 'gyur/ sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' rnams// sngags kyi spyod pa'i mchog bsgrub pas// rmongs pa 'da' bar bya na ni/ de'i srog ni der
25a8(rgyud): zad 'gyur/ de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin/ 'jig rten gsum gyi ston pa mchog/ 'jig rten gsum rdo rje gtsos/ gsung ni 'di skad bka' stsal to// sngag
25b1(rgyud): kyi skyes bu ji snyed pa// rdo rje gsum gyi ye shes rdzogs// dbang po gnyis kyi sbyor ba yi// dngos po thams cad rtag par bya/ 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad
25b2(rgyud): kyi// sngags kyi dam tshig bsgom pa'o// rig ma dbang phyug bzhugs pa la// rdo rje'i sbyor ba rab bsgom zhing // chags la chags pas blta bar bya// 'di ni
25b3(rgyud): dam tshig dkyil 'khor ro// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin/ de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi sras// thams cad dbang bskar sangs rgyas gtso// gsung ni 'di skad bka'
25b4(rgyud): stsal to// 'jig rten khams ni thams cad na// bud med ji snyed yod pa kun/ phyag rgya che sogs sbyor ba yis/ de dag thams cad nye bar spyad/ bye ba grangs
25b5(rgyud): med rdo rje 'dzin/ sangs rgyas ni der spro bya/ bcom ldan 'das byang chub kyi dam tshig gis de skad ces bka' stsal to// rdo rje gsum po mkha' 'dra ba'o// byang chub
25b6(rgyud): 'di yis thob par 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' rgyal rgya mtsho// rdo rje sems dpa' tshe nges thob// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi
25b7(rgyud): gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po bskul ba zhes bya ba'i le'u ste// // / bcu pa'o// // de nas
25b8(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i skyes bu mchog ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin
26a1(rgyud): la snyom par bzhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngags rdo rje rig pa'i skyes bu'i le'u 'di gsung so// rdo rje gsum yig sngags
26a2(rgyud): kyi mchog/ phyag rgya chen po rnam bsgom pa// byang chub thams cad thob pa'i phyir/ ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya/ oM ni ye shes snying po ste/ rdo rje'i sku ni thob byed
26a3(rgyud): pa'o// a ni byang chub bdag med pa/ rdo rje gsung ni thob byed pa'o// hUM ni sku gsung thugs yin te// rdo rje mi phyed gsum thob pa'o// bcom ldan 'das de bzhi
26a4(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi sngags kyi skyes bu'i de skad bka' stsal to// na mkha' rdo rje dbus gnas par// dkyil 'khor
26a5(rgyud): rdo rje kun bskyed bsam// rdo rje sprin ni 'phro bskyed pa// de ru yi ge b+h+rUM bas mo// de la ye shes rdo rje'i snying po'o// b+h+rUM rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par/ oM
26a6(rgyud): zhes bya ba rab tu bsgom// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// yi ge a ni rnam par bsam// chos kyi dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par/ yi ge
26a7(rgyud): hUM ni rab tu bsgom/ yi ge zla ni gnas bsgos te// rdo rje gsum 'byung bsgom par bya/ bcom ldan 'das dam tshig gsang bas de skad ces bka' stsal to// snying
26a8(rgyud): pi dus gsum sangs rgyas kyi// sku gsung thugs ni mazhes byed pa// oM ni sangs rgyas sku'i mchog/ yo// a ni sangs rgyas gsung gi lam/ a hU~M ni ye shes
26b1(rgyud): thugs kyi 'jing hUM// byang chub tshul mchog 'di yin te// 'di de sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sangs rgyas byang chub rab bsgrub pa// ye shes rdo rjes sprul
26b2(rgyud): pa ste// sangs rgyas rgya dang 'bras bu 'byung // 'di dag sangs rgyas skyes bu ste// sngags kyi rig pa zhes kyang bsgrags// rdo rje phyed gsum bsgom
26b3(rgyud): thig dam tshig dag gi rdzogs par 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs dam tshig de kho na nyid kyi ye shes rdo rje
26b4(rgyud): byin gyis brlob pa'i dpal zhes bya'i ting nge 'dzin to// dben zhing rab tu nyams dga' bA// sbyor ba 'di ni kun tsam na// rdo rje'i skra dang gsung dang
26b5(rgyud): thugs// zla ba phyed kyi nges par 'grub// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa ni// na mkha' rdo rje dbus bsam te// rang gi sngag gi dam tshig bskyed/ yi ge
26b6(rgyud): oM ni snying khar bzhag/ 'od zer lnga'i sprin chen po/ rnam par snang mdzad mchog tu bsgom// 'di yis sangs rgyas rnams kyi sku// rdo rje rnam snang rgya mtshor
26b7(rgyud): 'gyur// ye shes lnga ldan brten na ni// sangs rgyas sku na 'dra ba'i mdog/ rdo rje bskal pa gsum du ni// zla ba phyed kyi 'grub par 'gyur/ bcom ldan
26b8(rgyud): 'das sku rdo rje gsang bas de skad ces bka' stsal to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku/ rdo rje 'od zer bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to//
27a1(rgyud): chos kyi 'khor lo dam pa ni// nam mkha' rdo rje dbus su bsam/ rang gi sngags kyi skyes bu skyed// a ni ngag gi lam bzhag/
27a2(rgyud): ste/ kha dog lnga ni pad+ma che/ 'jig rten dbang mchog bsgom pa yis// dam tshig ye shes rdzogs byas te// tshig gi dam tshig lnga'i mchog/ chos
27a3(rgyud): kyi tshig gi lam gnas pa// rdo rje'i chos dang tshungs par 'gyur// ye shes lnga ldan brten na ni// rdo rje bskal pa gsum du gnas// bcom ldan 'das rdo
27a4(rgyud): rje'i gsung bsang bas de skad ces bka' stsal to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung rdo rje'i dam tshig 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to//
27a5(rgyud): rdo rje dkyil 'khor dam pa ni// na mkha'i rdo rje dbu su bsam// rang sngags skyes bu rdzogs byas la/ sems la yi ge hUM gnas pa// dam tshig chen po de nyid ni// /
27a6(rgyud): kha dog rnam sngar bsgom par bya// rdo rje kun dang rgyal ba'i gnas// ye shes rdo rje dag gi bya// ston pa rdo rje'i thugs 'dra ba// ye shes yon tan rgya mtshor 'gyur//
27a7(rgyud): ye shes lnga ldan brten na ni// rdo rje bskal pa gsum du gnas/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje'i thugs gsang bas de skad ces bka' stsal to// de bzhin gash+ye
27a8(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs dam tshig rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// ye shes dkyil 'khor dbu su ni// rdo rje chen po bsgom par
27b1(rgyud): bya/ lus dang kun la khang dmigs na/ rdo rje ye shes mkha' mnyam 'gyur// khaM sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' yis// yang nas yang du mchod
27b2(rgyud): pa dang // bskal pa gsum du dam tshig gnas// sangs rgyas kyis kyang gzigs mi 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das namakha'i rdo rje'i dam tshig gis de skad
27b3(rgyud): ces bka' stsal to// sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje mi snang ba 'byung ba bkod pa phreng ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// rdo rje dkyil 'khor dbu su ni/
27b4(rgyud): rang sngags skyes bu rab bsams la/ snying khar rdo rje haM zhes pa// bzhag ste 'od zer rnam par bsgom// haM/ 'jam dpal dam tshig longs spyod pa// sku
27b5(rgyud): gsung thugs kyi rdo rje ce na// sa bcu dag la gnas pa'i// byang chub sems dpar de 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi dam tshig rdo rje zla ba zhes
27b6(rgyud): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// 'od zer 'bar ba'i yi ge 'thing // na mkha'i dbyings dbus su bsam/ mtshon mchog rdo rje'i lus ngag gi/ rdo rje'i sku dang 'dra
27b7(rgyud): bar 'gyur/ b+h+r-ing // nam mkha'i rdo rje'i dam tshig gi bkod pa'i gnas zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// sangs rgyas mngon shes dam tshig mchog/ rdo rje 'chang
27b8(rgyud): dang 'dra bar 'gyur/ 'di ni dngos grub thams cad kyi// sangs rgyas mngon shes mchog bsgrub pa'o// namakha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// sangs
28a1(rgyud): rgyas dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// rdo rje sems dpa' rab bsgom la// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par/ ye shes oM ni bsgom par bya
28a2(rgyud): mo// rdo rje dam tshig gsum bsgom pas// mi bskyod rdo rje gsum 'drar 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje mi bskyod pas 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// mi bskyod
28a3(rgyud): ba'i sku 'dra dang // gsung dang thugs mchog 'dra ba 'dzin// 'jig rten khams rnams thams cad du/ mi bskyod rdo rjes mchod par 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'ad
28a4(rgyud): mi bskyod pa'i sku dang mnyam par mngon par 'byung ba'i dam tshig rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus su ni// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor
28a5(rgyud): 'od bzangs bsam// nam mkha'i rdo rje rab bsgom la// rin chen oM ni bsam par bya/ oM/ rdo rje dam tshig gsum bsgom pas// rdo rje gsum gyi dpal 'drar 'gyur
28a6(rgyud): lus dang ngag sems rdo rje yi// dkon mchog dpal gyi 'od dang 'dra/ de ni bdag med byang chub dang // ye shes gsang ba 'dra gnas 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das de
28a7(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa dkon mchog dpal gyis de skad bka' stsal to// rin po che dam tshig longs spyod rdo rje tshul zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi
28a8(rgyud): dbus ni/ sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor rnam pa bsam// 'jig rten dbang phyug rab bsgom la// chos kyi oM ni bsgoms par bya/ oMHrdo rje dam tshig gsum
28b1(rgyud): bsgoms pas// rdo rje gsum dpag med 'drar 'gyur// lus dang ngag sems rdo rje yis// 'od dpag med dang 'dra bar 'gyur// de ni sems can thams
28b2(rgyud): cid kyi// theg chen lam ni 'byung bar 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'od dpag med pas de skad ces bka' stsal to// yon tan dpag tu med pa'i rdo rje'i
28b3(rgyud): 'od kyi dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbu su ni/ sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// rdo rje ud pa la bsgom la// daM
28b4(rgyud): tshig oM ni rab tu bsgom// oM/ rdo rje dam tshig gsum bsgom pas// rdo rje gdon mi za 'drar 'gyur// lus dang ngag sems rdo rje yis// rdo rje thog med 'dra
28b5(rgyud): ba'i 'od/ de ni dpal ldan ye shes mtsho// sems can kun don 'byung bar 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gdon mi za ba'i de skad ces bka' stsal to// /
28b6(rgyud): gdon mi za ba'i dam tshig 'od zer ye shes kyi mchog 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// namakha'i dbyings kyi dbus su ni/ sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor
28b7(rgyud): dam pa bsam// rdo rje snang mdzad rab bsgom la/ sku gsum oM ni rab tu bsgom// oM/ rdo rje dam tshig gsum bsgoms pas// rnam par snang mdzad ma
28b8(rgyud): par 'gyur/ lus dang ngag yid rdo rje yis/ rnam par snang mdzad 'dra ba'i 'od// de ni ye shes rdzogs byang chub/ sku gsum mi phyed bsgrub byed 'gyur//
29a1(rgyud): shA/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje rnam par snang mdzad de skad bka' stsal to// lus dang ngag dang yi dmigs pa// mngon par byang chub pa'i rdo rje
29a2(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// rnam par dben pa'i ri bo dang // klung dang 'bab chu rnams dang // dur gyi khrod la sogs pa yang // bsam gtan bsdus 'di
29a3(rgyud): dag bsgom// mi bskyod ye shes dag la sogs// rdo rje nakha'i dkyil du bsam// mngon shes lnga pa'i sbyor ba yi// sangs rgyas mchog gi gan su bsgom//
29a4(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das dam tshig chen po rdo rje mngon par mkhyen pas de skad bka' bstsal to// rdo rje chen po rtse lnga pa/ 'bar ba lnga yi rnam par brgyan// gnas
29a5(rgyud): lnga dag tu sbyor ba yi// rdo rje mngon shes 'dra bar 'gyur/ me stags mang po 'khrug pa yi// rang sngags 'khor lo bsgom par bya// rdo rje lnga yi sbyor ba yi//
29a6(rgyud): rdo rje mngon shes 'dra bar 'gyur// rdo rje na mkha'i dkyil nyid du/ 'khor lo sangs rgyas 'bar 'od 'dra/ sangs rgyas 'jug par rab bsgom na// sangs rgyas
29a7(rgyud): gnas dang 'dra bar 'gyur/ sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par/ bdag gi lus la snang mdzad bzhag/ snying mkhar yi ge oM bsam la// sdug
29a8(rgyud): dag rnam par shes pa bsgom/ 'gog pa'i rdo rje sems nyid du/ gang tshe de la skye 'gyur na/ sangs rgyas kun gyi mchog 'dzin pa// yid bzhin dpal ldan
29b1(rgyud): lta bur 'gyur/ sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// rdo rje mi skyod rab tu bsgom// snying khar yi ge hUM bsgo nas/ sems ni thig ler gyur par
29b2(rgyud): bzhag/ sangs dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// tshe dpag med pa rab tu bsgom// snying khar yi ge a bsam te/ rdo rje thig ler gyur pa bzhag/ 'di
29b3(rgyud): de dam tshig mchog yin te// rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms pa/ 'gog pa'i dam tshig ye shes te/ sangs rgyas dngos grub 'thob 'gyur ba'o// rdo rje nam
29b4(rgyud): mkha'i dkyil gnas par/ gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ lus ngag sems la yi ge oM/ bsam na de ni bskal par gnas// rdo rje na mkha'i
29b5(rgyud): dbyings gnas par// chos kyi dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ lus ngag sems la yi ge a/ bsam na de ni bskal par gnas// rdo rje namakha'i dbying
29b6(rgyud): gnas par// rdo rje dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/ lus ngag sems la yi ge hUM/ bsam na de ni bskal par gnas// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gsum
29b7(rgyud): gyi rtog pa'i dam tshig gis de skad ces bka' stsal to// sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje yi// rnal 'byor 'dir gyur phyin chad ni// klog gam yang na sems
29b8(rgyud): kyang rung / de yang rdo rje 'dzin 'drar 'gyur// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi gsang ba// gsang ba 'dus pa la
30a1(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig de kho na nyid rdo rje'i rig pa'i skyes bu'i mchog gi le'u ste// // bcu gcig
30a2(rgyud): pa'o// // de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin/ skyed pa ye shes mchog bsgrub pa/ dam tshig de nyid rdo rje gsum// rdo rje gsung gi bka' stsal pa/ mkha'
30a3(rgyud): dang mtshungs par mnyam 'gyur ba/ rnam par mi rtog ngo bo nyid/ chos rnams rang bzhin dag pa la// rol mo 'di dag rab tu bsgom/ dgon pa chen po
30a4(rgyud): sa phyogs bsam// me tog 'bras bu sogs pas brgyan// ri bo dben pa'i sa phyog su/ dngos grub thams cad bsdus pas bsgrub// maM/ lus dang ngag
30a5(rgyud): sems rdo rje la// rdo rje 'jam pa rab tu bsgom// lus dang ngag sems lnga sgrol bas// rdo rje 'jam pa 'dra bar 'gyur// dpag tshad brgya'i khyon tsam du/
30a6(rgyud): rje 'bar ba'i 'od dag gis/ rgyan rnams kun gyis brgyan pa yi/ dag pa'i bdag nyid snang bar 'gyur/ tshangs pa drag po la sogs lhas// nams kyang mthong
30a7(rgyud): bar mi nuso// rdo rje 'jam pa mchog gi dam tshig mi snang ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// rdo rje mi phyed gsum las phyung // gshang lci dam tshig lnga rnam ni//
30a8(rgyud): lcags gsum las byung ldan byas te/ khar bcug nas ni bsgom par bya/ sangs rgyas kun gyi mi phyed pa'i// thugs ni de ni de ru rab bsgom na// rdo rje
30b1(rgyud): 'jam pa'i 'od 'dra bar/ de ma thag tu de 'gyuro// 'khor lo 'od 'phro mdangs mchog can// rang gyi sngags kyi rab bsgom nas// sangs rgyas thams
30b2(rgyud): cad bzhugs pa'i gnas// bsgom na sangs rgyas 'dra bar 'gyur// ri rab sum cu rtsa drug gi/ rdul phran ji snyed yod pa yi// rdo rje 'dzin dang 'dra ba kun// de'i
30b3(rgyud): rjesu 'brang bar 'gyur/ 'khor lo'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// rdo rje chen po rang sngags kyis// dkyil 'khor chen po dbus su rab bsgom
30b4(rgyud): latardo rje kun gyi gnas yin par// bsams na rdo rje 'dra bar 'gyur// ri rab sum bcu rtsa drug gi/ rdul phran ji snyed yod yod pa yi// de snyed kyi ni bud
30b5(rgyud): med rnams// yon tan can gyi gan su 'gyur/ drag po dag gi phyag byas pa/ khams gsum rdo rje chen por 'gyur/ rdo rje dam tshig ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin
30b6(rgyud): to// pad+mo chen po 'dab brgyad pa// rang sngags rdo rje bsam nas su// chos rnams kun gyi gnas yin par// bsam na chos dang 'dra bar 'gyur// ri rab/
30b7(rgyud): sum cu rtsa drug gi/ rdul phran ji snyed yod pa yi// sangs rgyas chod/ mchog dkyil 'khor du/ dag pa'i bdag nyid 'jog par byed// pad+mo mnyam pa nyid ni
30b8(rgyud): bya ba'i tingange 'dzin to// ye shes lnga ldan rab brten na/ bskal pa gsum gyi yum du gnas// phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ gsang ba gsum
31a1(rgyud): / la bstan bkur byed// 'od zer lnga'i mdog 'dra'i 'od// rang gi sngags kyi ral gri bsgom// mi ga yang lag na thog na ni// rdo rje
31a2(rgyud): gsum rig 'dzin par 'gyur// khams gsum kun gyi rab mchod cing // tshangs dbang lha min phyag byas pa// stong gsum na ni gcig pu pa// mi mchog gsang
31a3(rgyud): ba 'dzin par 'gyur// gang rnams 'dod dang bsam pa dag/ sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje'i thugs las rab tu byung // de lta bu'i dngos grub
31a4(rgyud): gter// ral gri thams cad kyi dam pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// oM ni ri lu tsi na kir/ 'bru chad tsam du bsam nas ni// dbusu rang gi lha'i gzugs/
31a5(rgyud): bsam te khar cug rnams bsgom na/ de ni de ma thag tu yang / byang chub sems dpo'i 'od 'drar 'gyur/ nyi ma shar ba'i 'od 'dra zhing // 'dzam bu'i chu bo
31a6(rgyud): gser gyi mdog/ a ni ri lu tsa la ka'i// 'bru chad tsam du bsam nas ni/ dbus su rang gi lha'i gzugs// bsam te khar cug rnam sgom na/ de ni de ma thag
31a7(rgyud): tu yang // byang chub ye shes 'o 'drar 'gyur/ nyi ma ma shar ba'i 'od 'dra zhing // 'dzam bu'i chu bo gser gyi mdog hUM ni ri lu tsa na ka'i// 'bru chad tsam du bas
31a8(rgyud): nas nas ni// dbus su rang gi lha'i gzugs// bsams te khar cug rnam bsgoms na/ de ni de ma thag tu yang // rdo rje sku dang 'od 'drar 'gyur// mkha' dbyings
31b1(rgyud): gsal ba'i dkyil gnas par// rnam par snang mdzad rab tu bsgom// lag tu 'khor lo rab bsgom na/ 'khor lo rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur/ 'khor lo/
31b2(rgyud): chen po'i rigs bsgoms te/ sangs rgyas sku ni rab sbyor zhing // ye shes 'di ni rab bsgrub pa'o// ye shes rdo rje dag gi bya// mkha' dbyings rdo rje dbus
31b3(rgyud): gnas pA/ ye shes mi bskyod rab bsgoms te// lag tu rdo rje rab bsgoms na// rdo rje rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// rdo rje chen po'i rigs bsgoms te// rdo rje skur
31b4(rgyud): ni rab sbyor zhi// rdo rje mchog 'di bsgrub pa 'di/ ye shes rdo rje dag gi bya// mkha' dbyings rin chen dbusta gunas pAR+Sha// rin chen rdo rje rab tu bsgom/
31b5(rgyud): lag tu rin chen rab bsgom na// rin chen rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// rin po che'i rigs bsgoms na// rin chen mchog 'di bsgrub pa yi// ye shes rdo
31b6(rgyud): rje dag gi bya// mkha' dbyings chos kyi dbyings gnas par/ tshe dpag med par rab tu bsgom/ lag tu pad+mo rab bsgom na/ pad+ma'i rigs pa 'dzin pa
31b7(rgyud): 'gyur/ pad+mo'i rin chen bsgom nas su// chos kyi sku ni rab sbyor zhing // pad+mo'i mchog 'di bsgrub pa ni/ ye shes rdo rje dag gI bya// mkha' dbyings dam tshig
31b8(rgyud): dbus gnas par/ gdon mi za ba'i ye shes bsgom/ lag tu ral gri rab bsgom na/ ral gro'i rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur/ dam tshig chen po'i rigs
32a1(rgyud): bsgoms te/ thob med dam tshig rab sbyor zhing // dam tshig mchog 'di bsgrub pa ni ye shes rdo rje dag gi bya/ rtse gsum ye shes lhag
32a2(rgyud): kyu sogs// rdo rje'i khyad par gyi bsgrub na// sku gsung thugs kyi bsgrub pa yis/ bsam gtan de ni 'grub par 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das dam tshig chen po
32a3(rgyud): dngos grub rdo rjes de skad bka' stsal to/ lam gyi bzhi mdo 'am shing gcig drung // mtshan ma gcig dang zhi gnas su// rdo rje dgug pa'i khyad par gyi//
32a4(rgyud): bsgrub pa po'i ni rtag tu bsgrub/ sbyor gsum rdo rje can rnams kyi// sbyor gsum sngags kyis bu bsam// sangs rgyas ye shes blo ldan gyis// sku gsung
32a5(rgyud): thugs kyi kyo ba btang // rlung gi dkyil 'khor mchog gnas pa// sangs rgyas dbug pa dam pa yin/ dam tshig las byung phyogs bcu pa// rdo rjes bkug
32a6(rgyud): nas nye bar spyod// na mkha' dbyings kyi dam tshig rdo rje dgug pa'i cho ga'o// rnam par snang mdzad mkhor lo che// rdo rje pad+ma la sogs pas// rgyal nas lcag sgyu
32a7(rgyud): bsam nas ni/ dam tshig mgugs mchog skyo bas bya// khams gsum gyi dam tshig mgugs pa'o// rnam pa mchog rnams kun ldan pa'i// sangs rgyas
32a8(rgyud): sku ni rnams bsgom la// lag tu sku dang gsung thugs kyi// kyo ba la sogs rab tu bsgom// 'di lta bu'i sbyor ba yis/ de ni gnas las byed par 'gyur/
32b1(rgyud): rnam pa mchog rnams kun ldan pa'i// rdo rje'i sku ni rnams bsgom la/ rdo rje'i sbyor bas lce bsgoms na// rdo rje'i gsung dang 'dra bar 'gyur/ rnam pa'i mchog
32b2(rgyud): rnams kun ldan pa'i// sangs rgyas skur ni rnam bsgoms la// lag tu bsgrub bya bsams na ni// rdo rje dang ni 'dra bar 'gyur/ gsang gsum dam tshig mchod pa'i mchog
32b3(rgyud): mchod pas mchod nas rab tu bsgrub// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyis// gsang ba'i snying po bsdus pa yin/ bcom ldan 'das gsang ba chen po'i dam tshig gi
32b4(rgyud): de skad bka' stsal to// sha chen dam tshig mchog gi ni// rdo rje gsum mchog bsgrub par// gshang lci dam tshig mchog gis ni/ rig pa 'dzin pa'i gtso bor 'gyur/
32b5(rgyud): glang po'i sha'i dam tshig gi/ mngon shes lnga dag thob par 'gyur// rta sha dag gi dam tshig gri/ mi snang ba'i bdag por 'gyur// khyi sha dag gi dam tshig gis// /
32b6(rgyud): dngos grub thams cad thob par 'gyur// ba glang sha'i dam tshig gis// rdo rje dgug pa'i mchog tu 'gyur// sha rnams thams cad med na yang // thams cad bsam
32b7(rgyud): pas rnam par brtag/ rdo rje'i sbyor ba 'di byas na/ sangs rgyas thams cad byin gyis brlob/ rnam pa mchog rnams kun ldan pa/ sku gsung thugs ni rdo rje can/
32b8(rgyud): snying khar ye shes dam tshig dang // dbu brgyan rdo rje mchog 'dzin pa// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyes 'gyur ba/ dam tshig mchog gi bya ba ni/ dngos grub
33a1(rgyud): thams cad 'grub pa'i mchog/ dam tshig mchog gi rab tu bya/ dam tshig thams cad ye shes rdo rjer 'gyur ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to//
33a2(rgyud): lce'i dam tshig rdo rje mchog/ rdo rje can gyi hUM bsgoms te/ bdud rtsi lnga yi sbyor ba yi/ zos na rdo rje gsum thob 'gyur/ a dang oM gyi dam tshig kyang /
33a3(rgyud): 'di ni rdo rje'i tshul mchog ste/ 'di lta bu yi sbyor ba yis// rdo rje mi phyed 'dra bar 'gyur// rdo rje'i dam tshig bdud rtsi'i phreng ba zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin to//
33a4(rgyud): rje dam tshig gsum bsgrub mchog/ sku gsum rdo rje can du 'gyur/ phyogs bcu'i sems can thams cad kyi// nor bu yid bzhin rgya mtshor 'gyur/ 'jig rten
33a5(rgyud): khams ni thams cad du/ rdo rje'i bdag nyid snang byed/ 'khor lo'i dam tshig gsum grub mchog/ sangs rgyas sku dang 'dra bar 'gyur/ gang gi bye
33a6(rgyud): snyed thams cad du/ grub pa kun tu rnam par spyod/ dam tshig dam pa thams cad kyi/ rig pa 'dzin pa'i gtso bar 'gyur// rdo rje'i sku ni rab bsgom
