33a7(rgyud): pas// thams cad dam tshig mchog tu 'grub/ mi snang gyur pa thams cad la// stong khams dag ni snang bar byed// sangs rgyas kun las 'phro ba dang /

33b1(rgyud): mthong bar 'gyur// gang gi'i bye snyed zhing rnams na// sgra brags pa ni ji snyed pa// mngon shes snabs thos pa ni/ rna ba'i drung na 'khod pa bzhin//
33b2(rgyud): gang ga'i bye snyed zhing dag gi// sems can kun gyi sems rnams ni/ sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan pa yi// rol mo las byung sems rig 'gyur//
33b3(rgyud): bskal pa gang gi'i bye snyed du// 'khor ba dag na gnas pa yi// sngon gyi gnas kyi gtan tshig rnams// zhag gsum lon pa bzhin du dran// gang gi
33b4(rgyud): bye ma snyed kyi lus// sangs rgyas sprin la sogs brgyan pas// bskal pa gang ga'i bye snyed du// rdo rje rdzu 'phrul mchog gi 'gengs// bcom ldan 'das
33b5(rgyud): dam tshig mngon par mkhyen de skad bka' stsal to// de la mngon par shes pa lnga ni// rdo rje'i spyan dang // rdo rje'i snyan dang / rdo rje'i thugs dang / rdo rje'i
33b6(rgyud): gnas dang // rdo rje'i rdzu 'phrul lo// sangs rgyas mngon shes lnga don grub// sa d+yas skra dang 'dra bar 'gyur/ gang ga'i bye snyed grangs med pa'i/
33b7(rgyud): 'khor gyi yongasu bsko nas su/ rdo rje'i skra dang gsung gyi thugs kyi// 'jig rten khams kun bgrod par 'gyur// bstan pa'i dam tshig sbyor ba dang //
33b8(rgyud): nye bar bsgrub pa 'byung ba dang / bsgrub pa'i don gyi dam tshig dang / bsgrub pa chen po dag dang bzhi/ rdo rje'i bye brag shes byas la/ de nas las/
34a1(rgyud): rnams bsgrub par bya/ bstan pa'i ting 'dzin rab sbyor ba// byang chub mchog ni bsgom par bya/ nye bar grub pa grub mchog la// rdo rje'i
34a2(rgyud): skye mched rnam pa spyad/ sngags kyi bdag po bsgom pa yis/ bsgrub pa'i tshe na bskul bar gsung // bsgrub pa chen po byed par gsung // sgrub pa

34b2(rgyud): yul lo// chos kyi gsung lam dpal dang ldan// rdo rje phyed gsum phyed pa/ byin gyis brlab kyi gnas byas te/ rdo rje sku dang ldan par bya// rdo rje mi

36a6(rgyud): 'khor grags// sngags kyi yi ge'i tshig thos pa// de ni khro bos zlas par bshad// 'dod pa'i don gyis myos gyur par// kun tu skyob cing phan par dga'

36a8(rgyud): sems can 'dod chags tshor gnas bzhag/ de ni 'dod chags bzlas par bshad// zhe sdang rdo rje las byung ste/ lus dang ngags la gnas pa'i// sem
36b1(rgyud): can zhe sdang la gnas bzhag/ de ni zhe sdang bzlas par bshad// dam tshig de nyid rdo rje gsum// dbu ma dam tshig rdo rje can/ de nyid dam tshig rdo rje yi//

36b3(rgyud): byang chub rdzogs par mdzad/ rig pa chen mo spyan la sogs// rtag tu 'dod pa'i don brtson pa// 'dod pa'i longs spyod dag gi ni/ ji ltar 'dod pa

36b6(rgyud): ldan 'das skyes bu chen po'i dam tshig gis de skad ces bka' stsal to// ye shes 'khor lo can rnams kyi/ 'khor lo snying kha'i dbus su bsgom// gsal

55b2(rgyud): 'dod pa yi// bud med rnyed na cho ga bzhin// dben par mchod pa brtsam par bya// gsang ba blang nas bza' bar bya// de ni de ma thag tu yang // 'jam dpal dang
55b3(rgyud): ni gzi brjid mnyam// mi snang bdag po dpal dang ldan// 'dzam bu ser gyi mdangs 'drar 'gyur// bshang ba'am yang na bza' ba 'am// sha dag kyang ni
55b4(rgyud): gzhug par bya// cho ga bzhin du sngags nas ni// zos na sangs rgyas kyis mi mthong // bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang chen po'i de skad bka' stsal to// bshang
55b5(rgyud): pa che ge bzhi ni blang nas ni// khams phor sbar mar bzhag par bya// brgya rtsa brgyad du bskul na ni// sangs rgyas nyi mas mi mthong ngo // khyi'i sha dang rta sha da
55b6(rgyud): sha chen dag ni cho ga bzhin// blangs nas sbyor ba'i thabs kyis ni// zos na de yi mi mthong ngo // bshang dang lhan cig sbyar ba yis// ri lu lcug gsum gyis
55b7(rgyud): bkris pa// dbang po gnyis kyi sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas kun gyi mi mthong ngo // khyi'i sha dang sbyar ba yi// ri lu lcags gsum gyis bkris pa// dbang po
55b8(rgyud): gnyis kyi sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas kun gyi mi mthong ngo // sha chen dang ni sbyar ba yi// ri lu gsum gyi bkris pa yi// dbang po gnyis kyi sbyor ba yi/
56a1(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun gyis mi mthong ngo // ba lang sha dang sbyar ba yis// ri lu lcags gsum gyi bukris pa// dbang po gnyis kyi sbyor ba yi/

56a3(rgyud): kun gyi mi mthong ngo // ga bur can dran sbyar ba yi// ri lu lkugs gsum gyi bkris pa// dbang po gnyis kyi sbyor ba yi// sangs rgyas kun gyi mi ma
56a4(rgyud): dza// gi wang a ka rur sbyar ba'i// ri lu lcags gsum gyi bkris pa// dbang po gnyis kyi sbyor ba yis// rdo rje stob po cher 'gyur ro// ga bur gur gum sbyar
56a5(rgyud): ba yis// ri lu lcags gsum gyis bkris pa// dbang po gnyis kyi sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas kun gyi mi mthong ngo // rdo rje 'dzin pa gang yang rung // phyag rgya chen por
56a6(rgyud): byin brlabs nas// de ni de 'dra'i dpal ldan pa'i// stobs chen pha rol gnon pa ra/ 'gyur// dpag tshad bye ba rdzogs pa yi// steng du rdo rje 'gro bar 'gyur// stong gsum brje

56a8(rgyud): gonas pa la// stobs chen gyis ni 'dod pa bcas// bcom ldan 'das dam tshig sems dpa'i mi snang ba'i rdo rje chen pos de skad bka' stsal to// de nas sangs rgyas
56b1(rgyud): bya nas ston pa rdo rje 'jim/

57a2(rgyud): rab tu dben par nid// bsam gtan rdo rje rab bya ba// bzlas dang sngags kyi sbyor bas so// rdo rje sems dpa' la sogs kun// sngags kyi bsam gtan gyis bskul bas//

57a4(rgyud): du ni rigs rtago/ dbab pa'i cho ga thams cad ni// byas na gdon mi za bar 'gyur// bskul dang reng ba lha chen po// 'phags lam bzhi po dag kyang ni// rdo rje grub pa dag gis bya/
57a5(rgyud): de ltar byas na rtag par 'grub// bu mo lo grangs bcu gnyis pa 'am// khye'u lo grangs bcu gnyis pa 'am// mtshan nyid thams cad yongs rdzogs pa// gzung nas dbab

57a7(rgyud): yi ge'i tshig 'di rnam so// hUM ha a d+hi/ na mkha'i khams ni sems med cing / rtog pa thams cad rnams spangs dang // rdo rje sems dpa' dag nyid kyang /

57b1(rgyud): bar bshad// 'gul ba dang ni g.yo ba yin// 'di ni bskul ba thams cad kyi// gsang ba yin par rab tu bshad// khru gang 'am khru do 'am// khru brgyad tsam dum lnga

57b7(rgyud): sha chen gyis ni thams cad kyi// rdo rje las byung 'jig par bshad// 'di ni dgra rnams thams cad kyi// 'jig pa shin du mi zad yin// dgra'i gzugs brnyan byas nas ni//
57b8(rgyud): bshong lci dag gi chos mchog can// cher mo'i me la khros nas bsreg/ sangs rgyas dag kyang nges par 'jig chu bo'i 'gram gnyis sa'i kyang // dgra'i gzugs ba/
58a1(rgyud): byas na ni// til 'bru tsam gyi yan lag kun// dug las byung ba'i tsher ma yis// bskul ba'i tshig dang bcas pas dgang // sangs rgyas dag kyang
58a2(rgyud): nges par 'jig/ skye tshe lan tshwa 'bru mar dang // dug dang da d+hu ra dag gi/ sangs rgyas thams cad gsad pa la// 'di dag mchog tu 'gyur bar bshad/ sol khus gsher
58a3(rgyud): ba'i gos dag ni// gyon te sems ni khros nas su// rkang pas ling ka gnan na ni// srin po'i khyer bar gdon mi za// rus che khrag dang dug rnams kyi// gzugs
58a4(rgyud): brnyan rab tu byas na ni// rdo rje sems dpa' drag po yang // myur ba dag tu khyer bar 'gyur// ske tshe bshang lci sbyar ba yi// ling ka yongasu gang bar ni// blugs

58a8(rgyud): 'di ni bsod pa'i mchog yin no// rdo rje sems pa' khro bo che// rnam par bgrad pa 'jigs 'jigs blta// sta ri tho ba phyag na bsnams// bsams nas bas
58b1(rgyud): gtan rab tu bya// de la 'di ni drag po chen po khro bo'i dam tshig go// mkha' dbyings thams cad sangs rgyas kyis// yongasu gang bar rab tu bsgom// gdug pa
58b2(rgyud): de yis gsad par ni// bsam na de ma thag tu 'chi// sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' yi// yongasu gang bar bsgom nas ni// gdug pa'i sems dpa

59a1(rgyud): rdo/ rje'i sta ri la sogs pas// bshag cing btub par bsams na ni// sku gsung gi mchog sbyin pa// rdo rje sems dpa' drag po 'ang mchi//

59a8(rgyud): ba'i phreng can ni// rdo rgyus dag gam gsol bri// de la 'di ni klu khro bo bskul ba'i snying po'o// khaM mi zad par ni 'gyur ba'i dug/ rdo rje'i dbus na 'dug

62a1(rgyud): / rje su rtogs par bya'o// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'di lta dper na// na mkha' la rtag tu med// bltar mi snang ba de bzhin du/

62a3(rgyud): lus dang / ngag dang / sems dang // chos thams cad dang / rdo rje gnas pa'i dam tshig ni thams cad kyi rjesu song ba// ngo bo nyid gcig pa'i phyir te// 'di lta ste/ sems kyi

62a6(rgyud): gnas pa ma yin// gzugs kyi khams na gnas pa ma yin// gzugs med pa'i khams na gnas pa yang ma yin te// chos gang khams gsum na mi gnas pa de ni

64b1(rgyud): pa tu bye brag du ni nges par dbul// 'di ni sngags rnams thams cad kyi// sku'i rdo rje las dam tshig/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i dkyil 'khor ro//
